Nickel index of the Feynman diagram: e12|e3|33||:0B_bB_vv|0b_vV|Vv_vv|| 

Diagram symmetry factor: 1 

Diagram description start.

Propagators (lines) in the diagram: 
{'line 0': [(0, 1), ['b', 'B']], 'line 1': [(0, 2), ['v', 'v']], 'line 2': [(1, 3), ['v', 'V']], 'line 3': [(2, 3), ['V', 'v']], 'line 4': [(2, 3), ['v', 'v']]} 
Notation for line n: [(vertex_1, vertex_2), (field_flows_out_of_vertex_1, field_flows_into_vertex_2)]

Loops in the diagram for a given internal momentum: 
[('line 3', 'line 4'), ('line 0', 'line 1', 'line 2', 'line 3')] 

Momentum propagating along the lines: 
{'line 0': -k + p, 'line 1': k, 'line 2': -k + p, 'line 3': k - q, 'line 4': q}

Frequency propagating along the lines: 
{'line 0': w - w_k, 'line 1': w_k, 'line 2': w - w_k, 'line 3': w_k - w_q, 'line 4': w_q}

Diagram integrand: 
PVv(k - q, w_k - w_q, 7, 10)*PbB(-k, -w_k, 1, 4)*PvV(-k, -w_k, 5, 9)*Pvv(k, w_k, 2, 6)*Pvv(q, w_q, 8, 11)*vertex_factor_Bbv(-k, 4, 3, 5)*vertex_factor_Bbv(p, 0, 1, 2)*vertex_factor_Vvv(-k, 9, 10, 11)*vertex_factor_Vvv(-k + q, 7, 6, 8)

The calculation of the integrand is divided into two stages: 
1. The calculation of the tensor structure T_ij 
2. The calculation of the scalar part F 
See file General_notation.txt for details.

Expression for the scalar function F: 
D_v(k)*D_v(q)*alpha(nuo, k, w_k)*beta(nuo, k, w_k)**2*beta(nuo, q, w_q)*beta(nuo, k - q, w_k - w_q)*beta_star(nuo, k, w_k)*beta_star(nuo, q, w_q)/(xi(k, w_k)**3*xi(q, w_q)*xi(k - q, w_k - w_q)*xi_star(k, w_k)*xi_star(q, w_q))

Expression for the tensor function T_ij (numbers for vector indices instead of alphabetic [1]): 
((-mom(k, 6) + mom(q, 6))*kd(7, 8) + (-mom(k, 8) + mom(q, 8))*kd(7, 6))*(-kd(9, 10)*mom(k, 11) - kd(9, 11)*mom(k, 10))*(I*rho*H(k, 2, 6) + P(k, 2, 6))*(I*rho*H(q, 8, 11) + P(q, 8, 11))*(-A*kd(0, 2)*mom(p, 1) + kd(0, 1)*mom(p, 2))*(A*kd(4, 5)*mom(k, 3) - kd(4, 3)*mom(k, 5))*P(k, 1, 4)*P(k, 5, 9)*P(k - q, 7, 10)

Scalar part of the propagator product  in a Wolfram Mathematica-friendly format: 
PbB[-k, -w_k]*Pvv[k, w_k]*PvV[-k, -w_k]*PbB[k - q, w_k - w_q]*Pvv[q, w_q]

The diagram is UV-convergent: 
False

Diagram description end.

Preparation for numerical integration for the integrand's scalar part consists in carrying out a replacing of variables k, q --> B*k/nuo, B*q/nuo, after which UV-convergent part of the diagram is divided into a dimensional factor C_F and a function F1 depending only on uo and integration variables k and q: F = C_F*F1.

1. In case of UV-convergent diagrams UV-convergent part is equal to F.
1. In case of UV-divergent diagrams UV-convergent part is equal to F - F(B = 0) [1].

The expression for F1 after momentums replacing: F1 ==> C_F_lambda*F1(B = 0) + C_F_B*(F1 - F1(B = 0)).

4*pi**2*Cutoff**(-2*d - 4*eps + 8)*go**2*nuo/Cutoff**10 

The expression for common C_F_B after momentums replacing: 
4*pi**2*go**2*nuo**11*(B/nuo)**(-2*d - 4*eps + 8)/B**10 

Calculation of T_ij. 

For UV-divergent diagrams, the expression for T_ij after calculating tensor convolutions is calculated both in the case of the presence of an external field B and for B = 0. For UV-finite diagrams, there is an expression for T_ij only in the external field. 

1. Tensor structure without the presence of B field (Lambda part): 
I*A*k**2*rho*(A*d*k**3*z**2 - A*d*k**3 - 2*A*d*k**2*q*z**3 + 2*A*d*k**2*q*z + A*d*k*q**2*z**2 - A*d*k*q**2 - A*k**3*z**2 + A*k**3 + 2*A*k**2*q*z**3 - 2*A*k**2*q*z**2 - 2*A*k**2*q*z + 2*A*k**2*q + 2*A*k*q**2*z**3 - 3*A*k*q**2*z**2 - 2*A*k*q**2*z + 3*A*k*q**2 + 2*A*q**3*z**3 - 2*A*q**3*z + d*k**3*z**2 - d*k**3 - 2*d*k**2*q*z**3 + 2*d*k**2*q*z + d*k*q**2*z**2 - d*k*q**2 - k**3*z**2 + k**3 + 2*k**2*q*z**3 - 2*k**2*q*z**2 - 2*k**2*q*z + 2*k**2*q + 2*k*q**2*z**3 - 3*k*q**2*z**2 - 2*k*q**2*z + 3*k*q**2 + 2*q**3*z**3 - 2*q**3*z)*lcs(s, 0, 3)*mom(p, s)/(d*(-d*k**2 + 2*d*k*q*z - d*q**2 + k**2 - 2*k*q*z + q**2)) 

2. Tensor structure with the presence of B field (B part): 
I*A*k**2*rho*(-A*d*k**3*z**2*z_k**2 + A*d*k**3*z**2 + A*d*k**3*z_k**2 - A*d*k**3 + 2*A*d*k**2*q*z**3*z_k**2 - 2*A*d*k**2*q*z**3 - 2*A*d*k**2*q*z*z_k**2 + 2*A*d*k**2*q*z - A*d*k*q**2*z**2*z_k**2 + A*d*k*q**2*z**2 + A*d*k*q**2*z_k**2 - A*d*k*q**2 + 2*A*k**3*z**2*z_k**2 - 2*A*k**3*z**2 - 2*A*k**3*z_k**2 + 2*A*k**3 - 4*A*k**2*q*z**3*z_k**2 + 4*A*k**2*q*z**3 - 2*A*k**2*q*z**2 + 4*A*k**2*q*z*z_k**2 + 4*A*k**2*q*z*z_k*z_q - 4*A*k**2*q*z - 2*A*k**2*q*z_k**2 - 2*A*k**2*q*z_q**2 + 2*A*k**2*q + 2*A*k*q**2*z**3 + 2*A*k*q**2*z**2*z_k**2 - 4*A*k*q**2*z**2*z_k*z_q - 4*A*k*q**2*z**2 + 2*A*k*q**2*z*z_k**2 + 4*A*k*q**2*z*z_k*z_q + 2*A*k*q**2*z*z_q**2 - 2*A*k*q**2*z - 4*A*k*q**2*z_k**2 - 2*A*k*q**2*z_q**2 + 4*A*k*q**2 + 2*A*q**3*z**3 - 4*A*q**3*z**2*z_k*z_q + 2*A*q**3*z*z_k**2 + 2*A*q**3*z*z_q**2 - 2*A*q**3*z - d*k**3*z**2*z_k**2 + d*k**3*z**2 + d*k**3*z_k**2 - d*k**3 + 2*d*k**2*q*z**3*z_k**2 - 2*d*k**2*q*z**3 - 2*d*k**2*q*z*z_k**2 + 2*d*k**2*q*z - d*k*q**2*z**2*z_k**2 + d*k*q**2*z**2 + d*k*q**2*z_k**2 - d*k*q**2 + 2*k**3*z**2*z_k**2 - 2*k**3*z**2 - 2*k**3*z_k**2 + 2*k**3 - 4*k**2*q*z**3*z_k**2 + 4*k**2*q*z**3 - 2*k**2*q*z**2 + 4*k**2*q*z*z_k**2 + 4*k**2*q*z*z_k*z_q - 4*k**2*q*z - 2*k**2*q*z_k**2 - 2*k**2*q*z_q**2 + 2*k**2*q + 2*k*q**2*z**3 + 2*k*q**2*z**2*z_k**2 - 4*k*q**2*z**2*z_k*z_q - 4*k*q**2*z**2 + 2*k*q**2*z*z_k**2 + 4*k*q**2*z*z_k*z_q + 2*k*q**2*z*z_q**2 - 2*k*q**2*z - 4*k*q**2*z_k**2 - 2*k*q**2*z_q**2 + 4*k*q**2 + 2*q**3*z**3 - 4*q**3*z**2*z_k*z_q + 2*q**3*z*z_k**2 + 2*q**3*z*z_q**2 - 2*q**3*z)*lcs(s, 0, 3)*mom(p, s)/(-d**2*k**2 + 2*d**2*k*q*z - d**2*q**2 + 3*d*k**2 - 6*d*k*q*z + 3*d*q**2 - 2*k**2 + 4*k*q*z - 2*q**2)

The expression for T_ij in helical MHD (A = 1): 

1. Tensor structure without the presence of B field (Lambda part): 
I*k**2*rho*(2*d*k**3*z**2 - 2*d*k**3 - 4*d*k**2*q*z**3 + 4*d*k**2*q*z + 2*d*k*q**2*z**2 - 2*d*k*q**2 - 2*k**3*z**2 + 2*k**3 + 4*k**2*q*z**3 - 4*k**2*q*z**2 - 4*k**2*q*z + 4*k**2*q + 4*k*q**2*z**3 - 6*k*q**2*z**2 - 4*k*q**2*z + 6*k*q**2 + 4*q**3*z**3 - 4*q**3*z)*lcs(s, 0, 3)*mom(p, s)/(d*(-d*k**2 + 2*d*k*q*z - d*q**2 + k**2 - 2*k*q*z + q**2)) 

2. Tensor structure with the presence of B field (B part): 
I*k**2*rho*(-2*d*k**3*z**2*z_k**2 + 2*d*k**3*z**2 + 2*d*k**3*z_k**2 - 2*d*k**3 + 4*d*k**2*q*z**3*z_k**2 - 4*d*k**2*q*z**3 - 4*d*k**2*q*z*z_k**2 + 4*d*k**2*q*z - 2*d*k*q**2*z**2*z_k**2 + 2*d*k*q**2*z**2 + 2*d*k*q**2*z_k**2 - 2*d*k*q**2 + 4*k**3*z**2*z_k**2 - 4*k**3*z**2 - 4*k**3*z_k**2 + 4*k**3 - 8*k**2*q*z**3*z_k**2 + 8*k**2*q*z**3 - 4*k**2*q*z**2 + 8*k**2*q*z*z_k**2 + 8*k**2*q*z*z_k*z_q - 8*k**2*q*z - 4*k**2*q*z_k**2 - 4*k**2*q*z_q**2 + 4*k**2*q + 4*k*q**2*z**3 + 4*k*q**2*z**2*z_k**2 - 8*k*q**2*z**2*z_k*z_q - 8*k*q**2*z**2 + 4*k*q**2*z*z_k**2 + 8*k*q**2*z*z_k*z_q + 4*k*q**2*z*z_q**2 - 4*k*q**2*z - 8*k*q**2*z_k**2 - 4*k*q**2*z_q**2 + 8*k*q**2 + 4*q**3*z**3 - 8*q**3*z**2*z_k*z_q + 4*q**3*z*z_k**2 + 4*q**3*z*z_q**2 - 4*q**3*z)*lcs(s, 0, 3)*mom(p, s)/(-d**2*k**2 + 2*d**2*k*q*z - d**2*q**2 + 3*d*k**2 - 6*d*k*q*z + 3*d*q**2 - 2*k**2 + 4*k*q*z - 2*q**2)

Preparation for numerical integration for the integrand's tensor part consists in carrying out a replacing of variables k, q --> B*k/nuo, B*q/nuo, after which T_ij is divided into a dimensional factor C_T and a function T1_ij depending only on uo and integration variables: T_ij = C_T*T1_ij. 
For UV divergent diagrams, this procedure applies to both Lambda part of T_ij and to B part of T_ij.

The expression for T1_lambda_ij (Lambda part of T_1_ij) after momentums replacing: 
A*k**2*(A*d*k**3*z**2 - A*d*k**3 - 2*A*d*k**2*q*z**3 + 2*A*d*k**2*q*z + A*d*k*q**2*z**2 - A*d*k*q**2 - A*k**3*z**2 + A*k**3 + 2*A*k**2*q*z**3 - 2*A*k**2*q*z**2 - 2*A*k**2*q*z + 2*A*k**2*q + 2*A*k*q**2*z**3 - 3*A*k*q**2*z**2 - 2*A*k*q**2*z + 3*A*k*q**2 + 2*A*q**3*z**3 - 2*A*q**3*z + d*k**3*z**2 - d*k**3 - 2*d*k**2*q*z**3 + 2*d*k**2*q*z + d*k*q**2*z**2 - d*k*q**2 - k**3*z**2 + k**3 + 2*k**2*q*z**3 - 2*k**2*q*z**2 - 2*k**2*q*z + 2*k**2*q + 2*k*q**2*z**3 - 3*k*q**2*z**2 - 2*k*q**2*z + 3*k*q**2 + 2*q**3*z**3 - 2*q**3*z)/(d*(-d*k**2 + 2*d*k*q*z - d*q**2 + k**2 - 2*k*q*z + q**2)) 

The expression for C_lambda_T after momentums replacing: 
I*Cutoff**3*rho*lcs(s, 0, 3)*mom(p, s) 

The expression for T1_B_ij (B part of T_1_ij) after momentums replacing: 
A*k**2*(-A*d*k**3*z**2*z_k**2 + A*d*k**3*z**2 + A*d*k**3*z_k**2 - A*d*k**3 + 2*A*d*k**2*q*z**3*z_k**2 - 2*A*d*k**2*q*z**3 - 2*A*d*k**2*q*z*z_k**2 + 2*A*d*k**2*q*z - A*d*k*q**2*z**2*z_k**2 + A*d*k*q**2*z**2 + A*d*k*q**2*z_k**2 - A*d*k*q**2 + 2*A*k**3*z**2*z_k**2 - 2*A*k**3*z**2 - 2*A*k**3*z_k**2 + 2*A*k**3 - 4*A*k**2*q*z**3*z_k**2 + 4*A*k**2*q*z**3 - 2*A*k**2*q*z**2 + 4*A*k**2*q*z*z_k**2 + 4*A*k**2*q*z*z_k*z_q - 4*A*k**2*q*z - 2*A*k**2*q*z_k**2 - 2*A*k**2*q*z_q**2 + 2*A*k**2*q + 2*A*k*q**2*z**3 + 2*A*k*q**2*z**2*z_k**2 - 4*A*k*q**2*z**2*z_k*z_q - 4*A*k*q**2*z**2 + 2*A*k*q**2*z*z_k**2 + 4*A*k*q**2*z*z_k*z_q + 2*A*k*q**2*z*z_q**2 - 2*A*k*q**2*z - 4*A*k*q**2*z_k**2 - 2*A*k*q**2*z_q**2 + 4*A*k*q**2 + 2*A*q**3*z**3 - 4*A*q**3*z**2*z_k*z_q + 2*A*q**3*z*z_k**2 + 2*A*q**3*z*z_q**2 - 2*A*q**3*z - d*k**3*z**2*z_k**2 + d*k**3*z**2 + d*k**3*z_k**2 - d*k**3 + 2*d*k**2*q*z**3*z_k**2 - 2*d*k**2*q*z**3 - 2*d*k**2*q*z*z_k**2 + 2*d*k**2*q*z - d*k*q**2*z**2*z_k**2 + d*k*q**2*z**2 + d*k*q**2*z_k**2 - d*k*q**2 + 2*k**3*z**2*z_k**2 - 2*k**3*z**2 - 2*k**3*z_k**2 + 2*k**3 - 4*k**2*q*z**3*z_k**2 + 4*k**2*q*z**3 - 2*k**2*q*z**2 + 4*k**2*q*z*z_k**2 + 4*k**2*q*z*z_k*z_q - 4*k**2*q*z - 2*k**2*q*z_k**2 - 2*k**2*q*z_q**2 + 2*k**2*q + 2*k*q**2*z**3 + 2*k*q**2*z**2*z_k**2 - 4*k*q**2*z**2*z_k*z_q - 4*k*q**2*z**2 + 2*k*q**2*z*z_k**2 + 4*k*q**2*z*z_k*z_q + 2*k*q**2*z*z_q**2 - 2*k*q**2*z - 4*k*q**2*z_k**2 - 2*k*q**2*z_q**2 + 4*k*q**2 + 2*q**3*z**3 - 4*q**3*z**2*z_k*z_q + 2*q**3*z*z_k**2 + 2*q**3*z*z_q**2 - 2*q**3*z)/(-d**2*k**2 + 2*d**2*k*q*z - d**2*q**2 + 3*d*k**2 - 6*d*k*q*z + 3*d*q**2 - 2*k**2 + 4*k*q*z - 2*q**2) 

The expression for C_B_T after momentums replacing: 
I*B**3*rho*lcs(s, 0, 3)*mom(p, s)/nuo**3 

Diagram integrand calculation end.

Calculation of the final expression for the integrand. 

F ==> C_int_lambda*F1(B = 0)*T1_lambda_ij + C_int_B*(F1 - F1(B = 0))*T1_B_ij, 
where C_int_lambda = C_F_lambda*C_lambda_T and C_int_B = C_F_B*C_B_T.

Dimensional multiplier before UV-divergent part of the integrand (with symmetric coefficient), i.e. C_int_lambda: 
4*I*pi**2*Cutoff**(-2*d - 4*eps + 1)*go**2*nuo*rho*lcs(s, 0, 3)*mom(p, s)

Dimensional multiplier before UV-convergent part of the integrand (with symmetric coefficient), i.e. C_int_B: 
4*I*pi**2*B**(-2*d - 4*eps + 1)*go**2*nuo**(2*d + 4*eps)*rho*lcs(s, 0, 3)*mom(p, s)

The complete integrand without C_int_B, i.e. F1*T1_B_ij:
